                   ==>  MISSING_ELSE

179                     function automatic void record_reghier_map(uvm_reg_map _map); begin
180                        uvm_reg _regs[$], _reg;
181                        uvm_reg_field _fields[$], _field;
182                        uvm_mem _mems[$], _mem;
183                        int _handle;
184                        string _full_name, _address, _regid, _label_name;
185                        uvm_sequencer_base _sequencer;
186                        uvm_reg_map _parent_map;
187                        uvm_reg_block _parent_blk;
188                        uvm_reg_addr_t _base_addr;
189                        int _decl;
190                        bit _need_end_event;
191                        int g_policy_id[string]; 
192                     
193                        _need_end_event = 1'b0;
194                        _decl = 0;
195                        _full_name = _map.get_full_name();
196                        _handle = pli_reghier_begin_event(_full_name);
197                     
198                        _parent_map = _map.get_parent_map();
199                        _parent_blk = _map.get_parent();
200                     
201                        if(_parent_blk) 
202                           $sformat(_label_name, "MAP_%0d_%0d", _map.get_inst_id(), _parent_blk.get_inst_id());
203                        else
204                           $sformat(_label_name, "MAP_%0d_", _map.get_inst_id());
205                     
206                        pli_reghier_set_label(_handle, _label_name);
207                     
208                        pli_reghier_add_attribute_string(_handle, "name", _full_name);
209                        if(_parent_blk) begin
210                           if (!verdi_clp.is_verdi_trace_no_decl())
211                               _decl = record_reg_decl_name(_handle, "_parent_blk", "_map", _map.get_name());
212                        end
213                     
214                        if(_parent_map) begin
215                           pli_reghier_add_attribute_int(_handle, "parent_map_id", _parent_map.get_inst_id());
216                        end
217                     
218                        retrieve_reg_def_class("_map", _handle);
219                     
220                        pli_reghier_add_attribute_int(_handle, "bus_width_in_bytes", _map.get_n_bytes());
221                     
222                        _base_addr = _map.get_base_addr();
223                        pli_reghier_add_attribute_logic(_handle, "base_address",  _base_addr, "+radix+hex", $size(_base_addr));
224                     
225                        _sequencer = _map.get_sequencer();
226                     
227                        if(_sequencer !=null)
228                           pli_reghier_add_attribute_string(_handle, "sequencer", _sequencer.get_full_name());
229                     
230                        pli_reghier_end_event(_handle);
231                        
232                        _map.get_registers(_regs, UVM_NO_HIER);
233                     
234                        _need_end_event = 1'b0;
235                        if(_regs.size()>0) begin
236                           _need_end_event = 1'b1;
237                           _handle = pli_reghier_begin_event(_full_name);
238                           pli_reghier_set_label(_handle, _label_name);
239                           //pli_reghier_add_attribute_int(_handle, "inst_id", _map.get_inst_id());
240                        end
241                       
242                        while(_regs.size() > 0) begin
243                           uvm_reg_addr_t _addr, _offset;
244                           uvm_reg_map_info _map_info;
245                           string _right;
246                           uvm_map_access_recorder _inst;
247                     
248                           _reg = _regs.pop_front();
249                     
250                           if(_map) 
251                              _map_info = _map.get_reg_map_info(_reg, 0); 
252                           
253                           if(_map_info==null) 
254                              _map_info = retrieve_reg_map_info(_map, _reg);
255                     
256                           if(_map_info!=null && !_map_info.unmapped) begin
257                     
258                              _right = _reg.get_rights(_map);
259                     
260                              if(!g_policy_id.exists(_right)) begin
261                                 int _policy_size;
262                     
263                                 _policy_size = g_policy_id.size();
264                                 pli_reghier_add_attribute_string(_handle, $sformatf("policy_%0d", (_policy_size+1)), _right);
265                                 g_policy_id[_right] = _policy_size+1;
266                              end
267                              pli_reghier_add_attribute_int(_handle, $sformatf("reg_%0d_access_policy_id", _reg.get_inst_id()), g_policy_id[_right]);
268                     
269                              _addr = _reg.get_address(_map);
270                              _inst = uvm_map_access_recorder::get_inst();
271                              _inst.insert_register(_addr, _map.get_full_name(), _reg);
272                     
273                              pli_reghier_add_attribute_logic(_handle, $sformatf("reg_%0d_address", _reg.get_inst_id()),  _addr, "+radix+hex", $size(_addr));
274                     
275                              _offset = _reg.get_offset(_map);
276                              pli_reghier_add_attribute_logic(_handle, $sformatf("reg_%0d_offset", _reg.get_inst_id()), _offset, "+radix+hex", $size(_offset));
277                     
278                              _reg.get_fields(_fields);
279                              while(_fields.size() > 0) begin
280                           
281                                 _field = _fields.pop_front(); 
282                                 _right = _field.get_access(_map);
283                      
284                                 if(!g_policy_id.exists(_right)) begin
285                                    int _policy_size;
286                     
287                                    _policy_size = g_policy_id.size();
288                                    pli_reghier_add_attribute_string(_handle, $sformatf("policy_%0d", (_policy_size+1)), _right);
289                                    g_policy_id[_right] = _policy_size+1;
290                                 end
291                                 pli_reghier_add_attribute_int(_handle, $sformatf("field_%0d_access_policy_id", _field.get_inst_id()), g_policy_id[_right]);
292                           
293                              end
294                           end
295                        end
296                        
297                        if(_need_end_event==1'b1)
298                           pli_reghier_end_event(_handle);
299                        
300                        _map.get_memories(_mems, UVM_NO_HIER);
301                        _need_end_event =1'b0;
302                        if(_mems.size() > 0) begin
303                           _need_end_event =1'b1;
304                           _handle = pli_reghier_begin_event(_full_name);
305                           pli_reghier_set_label(_handle, _label_name);
306                           //pli_reghier_add_attribute_int(_handle, "inst_id", _map.get_inst_id());
307                        end
308                     
309                        while(_mems.size() > 0) begin
310                           uvm_reg_addr_t _addr, _offset;
311                           uvm_reg_map_info _map_info;
312                           uvm_map_access_recorder _inst;
313                     
314                           _mem = _mems.pop_front(); 
315                     
316                           if(_map)
317                              _map_info = _map.get_mem_map_info(_mem, 0);
318                     
319                           if(_map_info==null)
320                              _map_info = retrieve_mem_map_info(_map, _mem);
321                     
322                           if(_map_info!=null && !_map_info.unmapped) begin
323                              $sformat(_regid, "mem_%0d_access_policy", _mem.get_inst_id()); 
324                              pli_reghier_add_attribute_string(_handle, _regid, _mem.get_access(_map));
325                     
326                              _addr = _mem.get_address(0, _map); // base address
327                              _inst = uvm_map_access_recorder::get_inst();
328                              _inst.insert_register(_addr, _map.get_full_name(), _mem);
329                      
330                              $sformat(_regid, "mem_%0d_address", _mem.get_inst_id()); 
331                              pli_reghier_add_attribute_logic(_handle, _regid,  _addr, "+radix+hex", $size(_addr));
332                        
333                        
334                              _offset = _mem.get_offset(0, _map); // base offset 
335                              $sformat(_regid, "mem_%0d_offset", _mem.get_inst_id()); 
336                              pli_reghier_add_attribute_logic(_handle, _regid,  _offset, "+radix+hex", $size(_offset));
337                           end
338                        end
339                     
340                        if(_need_end_event==1'b1)
341                           pli_reghier_end_event(_handle);
342                     
343                     end
344                     endfunction

549                     function automatic void record_reghier_reg(uvm_reg _reg); begin
550                        uvm_reg _cur_reg;
551                        uvm_reg_file _parent_regfile;
552                        uvm_reg_block _parent_blk;

332                       logic [ 3:0] is_greater_vec;
333                       logic [31:0] operand_b_eq;

337                       //second == comparator for CLIP instructions
338                       always_comb begin

340        1/2     ==>      if (operator_i == ALU_CLIPU) operand_b_eq = '0;

345                       always_comb begin

348        1/1              unique case (operator_i)
349                           ALU_GTS,
350                           ALU_GES,
351                           ALU_LTS,
352                           ALU_LES,

364                             endcase
365                           end

367        1/1                default: ;

371                       // generate vector equal and greater than signals, cmp_signed decides if the
372                       // comparison is done signed or unsigned
373                       genvar i;
374                       generate
375                         for (i = 0; i < 4; i++) begin : gen_is_vec
376                           assign is_equal_vec[i] = (operand_a_i[8*i+7:8*i] == operand_b_i[8*i+7:i*8]);
377                           assign is_greater_vec[i] = $signed(
378                               {operand_a_i[8*i+7] & cmp_signed[i], operand_a_i[8*i+7:8*i]}
379                           ) > $signed(
380                               {operand_b_i[8*i+7] & cmp_signed[i], operand_b_i[8*i+7:i*8]}
381                           );
382                         end
383                       endgenerate
384                     
385                       // generate the real equal and greater than signals that take the vector
386                       // mode into account
387                       always_comb begin
388                         // 32-bit mode
389        1/1              is_equal[3:0] = {4{is_equal_vec[3] & is_equal_vec[2] & is_equal_vec[1] & is_equal_vec[0]}};
390        1/1              is_greater[3:0] = {4{is_greater_vec[3] | (is_equal_vec[3] & (is_greater_vec[2]
391                                                                 | (is_equal_vec[2] & (is_greater_vec[1]
392                                                                  | (is_equal_vec[1] & (is_greater_vec[0]))))))}};
393                     
394        1/1              case (vector_mode_i)
395                           VEC_MODE16: begin
396        0/1     ==>          is_equal[1:0]   = {2{is_equal_vec[0] & is_equal_vec[1]}};
397        0/1     ==>          is_equal[3:2]   = {2{is_equal_vec[2] & is_equal_vec[3]}};
398        0/1     ==>          is_greater[1:0] = {2{is_greater_vec[1] | (is_equal_vec[1] & is_greater_vec[0])}};
399        0/1     ==>          is_greater[3:2] = {2{is_greater_vec[3] | (is_equal_vec[3] & is_greater_vec[2])}};
400                           end
401                     
402                           VEC_MODE8: begin
403        0/1     ==>          is_equal[3:0]   = is_equal_vec[3:0];
404        0/1     ==>          is_greater[3:0] = is_greater_vec[3:0];
405                           end
406                     
407        1/1                default: ;  // see default assignment
408                         endcase
409                       end
410                     
411                       // generate comparison result
412                       logic [3:0] cmp_result;
413                     
414                       always_comb begin
415        1/1              cmp_result = is_equal;
416        1/1              unique case (operator_i)
417        0/1     ==>        ALU_EQ:                                 cmp_result = is_equal;
418        0/1     ==>        ALU_NE:                                 cmp_result = ~is_equal;
419        0/1     ==>        ALU_GTS, ALU_GTU:                       cmp_result = is_greater;
420        0/1     ==>        ALU_GES, ALU_GEU:                       cmp_result = is_greater | is_equal;
421        0/1     ==>        ALU_LTS, ALU_SLTS, ALU_LTU, ALU_SLTU:   cmp_result = ~(is_greater | is_equal);
422        0/1     ==>        ALU_SLETS, ALU_SLETU, ALU_LES, ALU_LEU: cmp_result = ~is_greater;
423        1/1                default:                                ;
424                         endcase
425                       end
426                     
427                       assign comparison_result_o = cmp_result[3];
428                     
429                     
430                       // min/max/abs handling
431                       logic [31:0] result_minmax;
432                       logic [ 3:0] sel_minmax;
433                       logic        do_min;
434                       logic [31:0] minmax_b;
435                     
436                       assign minmax_b = (operator_i == ALU_ABS) ? adder_result : operand_b_i;
437                     
438                       assign do_min   = (operator_i == ALU_MIN)  || (operator_i == ALU_MINU) ||
439                                         (operator_i == ALU_CLIP) || (operator_i == ALU_CLIPU);
440                     
441                       assign sel_minmax[3:0] = is_greater ^ {4{do_min}};
442                     
443                       assign result_minmax[31:24] = (sel_minmax[3] == 1'b1) ? operand_a_i[31:24] : minmax_b[31:24];
444                       assign result_minmax[23:16] = (sel_minmax[2] == 1'b1) ? operand_a_i[23:16] : minmax_b[23:16];
445                       assign result_minmax[15:8] = (sel_minmax[1] == 1'b1) ? operand_a_i[15:8] : minmax_b[15:8];
446                       assign result_minmax[7:0] = (sel_minmax[0] == 1'b1) ? operand_a_i[7:0] : minmax_b[7:0];
447                     
448                       //////////////////////////////////////////////////
449                       // Clip
450                       //////////////////////////////////////////////////
451                       logic [31:0] clip_result;  // result of clip and clip
452                     
453                       always_comb begin
454        1/1              clip_result = result_minmax;
455        1/1              if (operator_i == ALU_CLIPU) begin
456        0/1     ==>        if (operand_a_i[31] || is_equal_clip) begin
457        0/1     ==>          clip_result = '0;
458                           end else begin
459        0/1     ==>          clip_result = result_minmax;
460                           end
461                         end else begin
462                           //CLIP
463        1/1                if (adder_result_expanded[36] || is_equal_clip) begin
464        1/1                  clip_result = operand_b_neg;
465                           end else begin
466        1/1                  clip_result = result_minmax;
467                           end
468                         end
469                     
470                       end
471                     
472                       //////////////////////////////////////////////////
473                       //  ____  _   _ _   _ _____ _____ _     _____   //
474                       // / ___|| | | | | | |  ___|  ___| |   | ____|  //
475                       // \___ \| |_| | | | | |_  | |_  | |   |  _|    //
476                       //  ___) |  _  | |_| |  _| |  _| | |___| |___   //
477                       // |____/|_| |_|\___/|_|   |_|   |_____|_____|  //
478                       //                                              //
479                       //////////////////////////////////////////////////
480                     
481                       logic [3:0][1:0] shuffle_byte_sel;  // select byte in register: 31:24, 23:16, 15:8, 7:0
482                       logic [3:0]      shuffle_reg_sel;  // select register: rD/rS2 or rS1
483                       logic [1:0]      shuffle_reg1_sel;  // select register rD or rS2 for next stage
484                       logic [1:0]      shuffle_reg0_sel;
485                       logic [3:0]      shuffle_through;
486                     
487                       logic [31:0] shuffle_r1, shuffle_r0;
488                       logic [31:0] shuffle_r1_in, shuffle_r0_in;
489                       logic [31:0] shuffle_result;
490                       logic [31:0] pack_result;
491                     
492                     
493                       always_comb begin
494        1/1              shuffle_reg_sel  = '0;
495        1/1              shuffle_reg1_sel = 2'b01;
496        1/1              shuffle_reg0_sel = 2'b10;
497        1/1              shuffle_through  = '1;
498                     
499        1/1              unique case (operator_i)
500                           ALU_EXT, ALU_EXTS: begin
501        0/2     ==>          if (operator_i == ALU_EXTS) shuffle_reg1_sel = 2'b11;
                   ==>  MISSING_ELSE
502                     
503        0/1     ==>          if (vector_mode_i == VEC_MODE8) begin
504        0/1     ==>            shuffle_reg_sel[3:1] = 3'b111;
505        0/1     ==>            shuffle_reg_sel[0]   = 1'b0;
506                             end else begin
507        0/1     ==>            shuffle_reg_sel[3:2] = 2'b11;
508        0/1     ==>            shuffle_reg_sel[1:0] = 2'b00;
509                             end
510                           end
511                     
512                           ALU_PCKLO: begin
513        0/1     ==>          shuffle_reg1_sel = 2'b00;
514                     
515        0/1     ==>          if (vector_mode_i == VEC_MODE8) begin
516        0/1     ==>            shuffle_through = 4'b0011;
517        0/1     ==>            shuffle_reg_sel = 4'b0001;
518                             end else begin
519        0/1     ==>            shuffle_reg_sel = 4'b0011;
520                             end
521                           end
522                     
523                           ALU_PCKHI: begin
524        0/1     ==>          shuffle_reg1_sel = 2'b00;
525                     
526        0/1     ==>          if (vector_mode_i == VEC_MODE8) begin
527        0/1     ==>            shuffle_through = 4'b1100;
528        0/1     ==>            shuffle_reg_sel = 4'b0100;
529                             end else begin
530        0/1     ==>            shuffle_reg_sel = 4'b0011;
531                             end
532                           end
533                     
534                           ALU_SHUF2: begin
535        0/1     ==>          unique case (vector_mode_i)
536                               VEC_MODE8: begin
537        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg_sel[3] = ~operand_b_i[26];
538        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg_sel[2] = ~operand_b_i[18];
539        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg_sel[1] = ~operand_b_i[10];
540        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg_sel[0] = ~operand_b_i[2];
541                               end
542                     
543                               VEC_MODE16: begin
544        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg_sel[3] = ~operand_b_i[17];
545        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg_sel[2] = ~operand_b_i[17];
546        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg_sel[1] = ~operand_b_i[1];
547        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg_sel[0] = ~operand_b_i[1];
548                               end
549        0/1     ==>            default: ;
550                             endcase
551                           end
552                     
553                           ALU_INS: begin
554        0/1     ==>          unique case (vector_mode_i)
555                               VEC_MODE8: begin
556        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg0_sel = 2'b00;
557        0/1     ==>              unique case (imm_vec_ext_i)
558                                   2'b00: begin
559        0/1     ==>                  shuffle_reg_sel[3:0] = 4'b1110;
560                                   end
561                                   2'b01: begin
562        0/1     ==>                  shuffle_reg_sel[3:0] = 4'b1101;
563                                   end
564                                   2'b10: begin
565        0/1     ==>                  shuffle_reg_sel[3:0] = 4'b1011;
566                                   end
567                                   2'b11: begin
568        0/1     ==>                  shuffle_reg_sel[3:0] = 4'b0111;
569                                   end
570                                 endcase
571                               end
572                               VEC_MODE16: begin
573        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg0_sel   = 2'b01;
574        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg_sel[3] = ~imm_vec_ext_i[0];
575        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg_sel[2] = ~imm_vec_ext_i[0];
576        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg_sel[1] = imm_vec_ext_i[0];
577        0/1     ==>              shuffle_reg_sel[0] = imm_vec_ext_i[0];
578                               end
579        0/1     ==>            default: ;
580                             endcase
581                           end
582                     
583        1/1                default: ;
584                         endcase
585                       end
586                     
587                       always_comb begin
588        1/1              shuffle_byte_sel = '0;
589                     
590                         // byte selector
591        1/1              unique case (operator_i)
592                           ALU_EXTS, ALU_EXT: begin
593        0/1     ==>          unique case (vector_mode_i)
594                               VEC_MODE8: begin
595        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[3] = imm_vec_ext_i[1:0];
596        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[2] = imm_vec_ext_i[1:0];
597        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[1] = imm_vec_ext_i[1:0];
598        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[0] = imm_vec_ext_i[1:0];
599                               end
600                     
601                               VEC_MODE16: begin
602        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[3] = {imm_vec_ext_i[0], 1'b1};
603        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[2] = {imm_vec_ext_i[0], 1'b1};
604        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[1] = {imm_vec_ext_i[0], 1'b1};
605        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[0] = {imm_vec_ext_i[0], 1'b0};
606                               end
607                     
608        0/1     ==>            default: ;
609                             endcase
610                           end
611                     
612                           ALU_PCKLO: begin
613        0/1     ==>          unique case (vector_mode_i)
614                               VEC_MODE8: begin
615        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[3] = 2'b00;
616        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[2] = 2'b00;
617        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[1] = 2'b00;
618        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[0] = 2'b00;
619                               end
620                     
621                               VEC_MODE16: begin
622        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[3] = 2'b01;
623        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[2] = 2'b00;
624        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[1] = 2'b01;
625        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[0] = 2'b00;
626                               end
627                     
628        0/1     ==>            default: ;
629                             endcase
630                           end
631                     
632                           ALU_PCKHI: begin
633        0/1     ==>          unique case (vector_mode_i)
634                               VEC_MODE8: begin
635        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[3] = 2'b00;
636        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[2] = 2'b00;
637        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[1] = 2'b00;
638        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[0] = 2'b00;
639                               end
640                     
641                               VEC_MODE16: begin
642        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[3] = 2'b11;
643        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[2] = 2'b10;
644        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[1] = 2'b11;
645        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[0] = 2'b10;
646                               end
647                     
648        0/1     ==>            default: ;
649                             endcase
650                           end
651                     
652                           ALU_SHUF2, ALU_SHUF: begin
653        0/1     ==>          unique case (vector_mode_i)
654                               VEC_MODE8: begin
655        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[3] = operand_b_i[25:24];
656        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[2] = operand_b_i[17:16];
657        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[1] = operand_b_i[9:8];
658        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[0] = operand_b_i[1:0];
659                               end
660                     
661                               VEC_MODE16: begin
662        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[3] = {operand_b_i[16], 1'b1};
663        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[2] = {operand_b_i[16], 1'b0};
664        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[1] = {operand_b_i[0], 1'b1};
665        0/1     ==>              shuffle_byte_sel[0] = {operand_b_i[0], 1'b0};
666                               end
667        0/1     ==>            default: ;
668                             endcase
669                           end
670                     
671                           ALU_INS: begin
672        0/1     ==>          shuffle_byte_sel[3] = 2'b11;
673        0/1     ==>          shuffle_byte_sel[2] = 2'b10;
674        0/1     ==>          shuffle_byte_sel[1] = 2'b01;
675        0/1     ==>          shuffle_byte_sel[0] = 2'b00;
676                           end
677                     
678        1/1                default: ;
679                         endcase
680                       end
681                     
682                       assign shuffle_r0_in = shuffle_reg0_sel[1] ?
683                                               operand_a_i :
684                                               (shuffle_reg0_sel[0] ? {2{operand_a_i[15:0]}} : {4{operand_a_i[7:0]}});
685                     
686                       assign shuffle_r1_in = shuffle_reg1_sel[1] ? {
687                         {8{operand_a_i[31]}}, {8{operand_a_i[23]}}, {8{operand_a_i[15]}}, {8{operand_a_i[7]}}
688                       } : (shuffle_reg1_sel[0] ? operand_c_i : operand_b_i);
689                     
690                       assign shuffle_r0[31:24] = shuffle_byte_sel[3][1] ?
691                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[3][0] ? shuffle_r0_in[31:24] : shuffle_r0_in[23:16]) :
692                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[3][0] ? shuffle_r0_in[15: 8] : shuffle_r0_in[ 7: 0]);
693                       assign shuffle_r0[23:16] = shuffle_byte_sel[2][1] ?
694                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[2][0] ? shuffle_r0_in[31:24] : shuffle_r0_in[23:16]) :
695                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[2][0] ? shuffle_r0_in[15: 8] : shuffle_r0_in[ 7: 0]);
696                       assign shuffle_r0[15: 8] = shuffle_byte_sel[1][1] ?
697                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[1][0] ? shuffle_r0_in[31:24] : shuffle_r0_in[23:16]) :
698                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[1][0] ? shuffle_r0_in[15: 8] : shuffle_r0_in[ 7: 0]);
699                       assign shuffle_r0[ 7: 0] = shuffle_byte_sel[0][1] ?
700                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[0][0] ? shuffle_r0_in[31:24] : shuffle_r0_in[23:16]) :
701                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[0][0] ? shuffle_r0_in[15: 8] : shuffle_r0_in[ 7: 0]);
702                     
703                       assign shuffle_r1[31:24] = shuffle_byte_sel[3][1] ?
704                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[3][0] ? shuffle_r1_in[31:24] : shuffle_r1_in[23:16]) :
705                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[3][0] ? shuffle_r1_in[15: 8] : shuffle_r1_in[ 7: 0]);
706                       assign shuffle_r1[23:16] = shuffle_byte_sel[2][1] ?
707                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[2][0] ? shuffle_r1_in[31:24] : shuffle_r1_in[23:16]) :
708                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[2][0] ? shuffle_r1_in[15: 8] : shuffle_r1_in[ 7: 0]);
709                       assign shuffle_r1[15: 8] = shuffle_byte_sel[1][1] ?
710                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[1][0] ? shuffle_r1_in[31:24] : shuffle_r1_in[23:16]) :
711                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[1][0] ? shuffle_r1_in[15: 8] : shuffle_r1_in[ 7: 0]);
712                       assign shuffle_r1[ 7: 0] = shuffle_byte_sel[0][1] ?
713                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[0][0] ? shuffle_r1_in[31:24] : shuffle_r1_in[23:16]) :
714                                                   (shuffle_byte_sel[0][0] ? shuffle_r1_in[15: 8] : shuffle_r1_in[ 7: 0]);
715                     
716                       assign shuffle_result[31:24] = shuffle_reg_sel[3] ? shuffle_r1[31:24] : shuffle_r0[31:24];
717                       assign shuffle_result[23:16] = shuffle_reg_sel[2] ? shuffle_r1[23:16] : shuffle_r0[23:16];
718                       assign shuffle_result[15:8] = shuffle_reg_sel[1] ? shuffle_r1[15:8] : shuffle_r0[15:8];
719                       assign shuffle_result[7:0] = shuffle_reg_sel[0] ? shuffle_r1[7:0] : shuffle_r0[7:0];
720                     
721                       assign pack_result[31:24] = shuffle_through[3] ? shuffle_result[31:24] : operand_c_i[31:24];
722                       assign pack_result[23:16] = shuffle_through[2] ? shuffle_result[23:16] : operand_c_i[23:16];
723                       assign pack_result[15:8] = shuffle_through[1] ? shuffle_result[15:8] : operand_c_i[15:8];
724                       assign pack_result[7:0] = shuffle_through[0] ? shuffle_result[7:0] : operand_c_i[7:0];
725                     
726                     
727                       /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
728                       //   ____  _ _      ____                  _      ___               //
729                       //  | __ )(_) |_   / ___|___  _   _ _ __ | |_   / _ \ _ __  ___    //
730                       //  |  _ \| | __| | |   / _ \| | | | '_ \| __| | | | | '_ \/ __|   //
731                       //  | |_) | | |_  | |__| (_) | |_| | | | | |_  | |_| | |_) \__ \_  //
732                       //  |____/|_|\__|  \____\___/ \__,_|_| |_|\__|  \___/| .__/|___(_) //
733                       //                                                   |_|           //
734                       /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
735                     
736                       logic [31:0] ff_input;  // either op_a_i or its bit reversed version
737                       logic [ 5:0] cnt_result;  // population count
738                       logic [ 5:0] clb_result;  // count leading bits
739                       logic [ 4:0] ff1_result;  // holds the index of the first '1'
740                       logic        ff_no_one;  // if no ones are found
741                       logic [ 4:0] fl1_result;  // holds the index of the last '1'
742                       logic [ 5:0] bitop_result;  // result of all bitop operations muxed together
743                     
744                       cv32e40p_popcnt popcnt_i (
745                           .in_i    (operand_a_i),
746                           .result_o(cnt_result)
747                       );
748                     
749                       always_comb begin
750        1/1              ff_input = '0;
751                     
752        1/1              case (operator_i)
753        0/1     ==>        ALU_FF1: ff_input = operand_a_i;
754                     
755        1/1                ALU_DIVU, ALU_REMU, ALU_FL1: ff_input = operand_a_rev;
756                     
757                           ALU_DIV, ALU_REM, ALU_CLB: begin
758        1/2     ==>          if (operand_a_i[31]) ff_input = operand_a_neg_rev;
759        1/1                  else ff_input = operand_a_rev;
760                           end
                        MISSING_DEFAULT
761                         endcase
762                       end
763                     
764                       cv32e40p_ff_one ff_one_i (
765                           .in_i       (ff_input),
766                           .first_one_o(ff1_result),
767                           .no_ones_o  (ff_no_one)
768                       );
769                     
770                       // special case if ff1_res is 0 (no 1 found), then we keep the 0
771                       // this is done in the result mux
772                       assign fl1_result = 5'd31 - ff1_result;
773                       assign clb_result = ff1_result - 5'd1;
774                     
775                       always_comb begin
776        1/1              bitop_result = '0;
777        1/1              case (operator_i)
778        0/1     ==>        ALU_FF1: bitop_result = ff_no_one ? 6'd32 : {1'b0, ff1_result};
779        0/1     ==>        ALU_FL1: bitop_result = ff_no_one ? 6'd32 : {1'b0, fl1_result};
780        0/1     ==>        ALU_CNT: bitop_result = cnt_result;
781                           ALU_CLB: begin
782        0/1     ==>          if (ff_no_one) begin
783        0/2     ==>            if (operand_a_i[31]) bitop_result = 6'd31;
784        0/1     ==>            else bitop_result = '0;
785                             end else begin
786        0/1     ==>            bitop_result = clb_result;
787                             end
788                           end
789        1/1                default: ;
790                         endcase
791                       end
792                     
793                     
794                       ////////////////////////////////////////////////
795                       //  ____  _ _     __  __             _        //
796                       // | __ )(_) |_  |  \/  | __ _ _ __ (_)_ __   //
797                       // |  _ \| | __| | |\/| |/ _` | '_ \| | '_ \  //
798                       // | |_) | | |_  | |  | | (_| | | | | | |_) | //
799                       // |____/|_|\__| |_|  |_|\__,_|_| |_|_| .__/  //
800                       //                                    |_|     //
801                       ////////////////////////////////////////////////
802                     
803                       logic extract_is_signed;
804                       logic extract_sign;
805                       logic [31:0] bmask_first, bmask_inv;
806                       logic [31:0] bextins_and;
807                       logic [31:0] bextins_result, bclr_result, bset_result;
808                     
809                     
810                       // construct bit mask for insert/extract/bclr/bset
811                       // bmask looks like this 00..0011..1100..00
812                       assign bmask_first       = {32'hFFFFFFFE} << bmask_a_i;
813                       assign bmask             = (~bmask_first) << bmask_b_i;
814                       assign bmask_inv         = ~bmask;
815                     
816                       assign bextins_and       = (operator_i == ALU_BINS) ? operand_c_i : {32{extract_sign}};
817                     
818                       assign extract_is_signed = (operator_i == ALU_BEXT);
819                       assign extract_sign      = extract_is_signed & shift_result[bmask_a_i];
820                     
821                       assign bextins_result    = (bmask & shift_result) | (bextins_and & bmask_inv);
822                     
823                       assign bclr_result       = operand_a_i & bmask_inv;
824                       assign bset_result       = operand_a_i | bmask;
825                     
826                       /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
827                       //  ____ _____ _______     _____  ________      ________ _____   _____ ______  //
828                       // |  _ \_   _|__   __|   |  __ \|  ____\ \    / /  ____|  __ \ / ____|  ____| //
829                       // | |_) || |    | |______| |__) | |__   \ \  / /| |__  | |__) | (___ | |__    //
830                       // |  _ < | |    | |______|  _  /|  __|   \ \/ / |  __| |  _  / \___ \|  __|   //
831                       // | |_) || |_   | |      | | \ \| |____   \  /  | |____| | \ \ ____) | |____  //
832                       // |____/_____|  |_|      |_|  \_\______|   \/   |______|_|  \_\_____/|______| //
833                       //                                                                             //
834                       /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
835                     
836                       logic [31:0] radix_2_rev;
837                       logic [31:0] radix_4_rev;
838                       logic [31:0] radix_8_rev;
839                       logic [31:0] reverse_result;
840                       logic [ 1:0] radix_mux_sel;
841                     
842                       assign radix_mux_sel = bmask_a_i[1:0];
843                     
844                       generate
845                         // radix-2 bit reverse
846                         for (j = 0; j < 32; j++) begin : gen_radix_2_rev
847                           assign radix_2_rev[j] = shift_result[31-j];
848                         end
849                         // radix-4 bit reverse
850                         for (j = 0; j < 16; j++) begin : gen_radix_4_rev
851                           assign radix_4_rev[2*j+1:2*j] = shift_result[31-j*2:31-j*2-1];
852                         end
853                         // radix-8 bit reverse
854                         for (j = 0; j < 10; j++) begin : gen_radix_8_rev
855                           assign radix_8_rev[3*j+2:3*j] = shift_result[31-j*3:31-j*3-2];
856                         end
857                         assign radix_8_rev[31:30] = 2'b0;
858                       endgenerate
859                     
860                       always_comb begin
861        1/1              reverse_result = '0;
862                     
863        1/1              unique case (radix_mux_sel)
864        1/1                2'b00: reverse_result = radix_2_rev;
865        1/1                2'b01: reverse_result = radix_4_rev;
866        1/1                2'b10: reverse_result = radix_8_rev;
867                     
868        1/1                default: reverse_result = radix_2_rev;
869                         endcase
870                       end
871                     
872                       ////////////////////////////////////////////////////
873                       //  ____ _____     __     __  ____  _____ __  __  //
874                       // |  _ \_ _\ \   / /    / / |  _ \| ____|  \/  | //
875                       // | | | | | \ \ / /    / /  | |_) |  _| | |\/| | //
876                       // | |_| | |  \ V /    / /   |  _ <| |___| |  | | //
877                       // |____/___|  \_/    /_/    |_| \_\_____|_|  |_| //
878                       //                                                //
879                       ////////////////////////////////////////////////////
880                     
881                       logic [31:0] result_div;
882                       logic        div_ready;
883                       logic        div_signed;
884                       logic        div_op_a_signed;
885                       logic [ 5:0] div_shift_int;
886                     
887                       assign div_signed = operator_i[0];
888                     
889                       assign div_op_a_signed = operand_a_i[31] & div_signed;
890                     
891                       assign div_shift_int = ff_no_one ? 6'd31 : clb_result;
892                       assign div_shift = div_shift_int + (div_op_a_signed ? 6'd0 : 6'd1);
893                     
894                       assign div_valid = enable_i & ((operator_i == ALU_DIV) || (operator_i == ALU_DIVU) ||
895                                          (operator_i == ALU_REM) || (operator_i == ALU_REMU));
896                     
897                       // inputs A and B are swapped
898                       cv32e40p_alu_div alu_div_i (
899                           .Clk_CI (clk),
900                           .Rst_RBI(rst_n),
901                     
902                           // input IF
903                           .OpA_DI      (operand_b_i),
904                           .OpB_DI      (shift_left_result),
905                           .OpBShift_DI (div_shift),
906                           .OpBIsZero_SI((cnt_result == 0)),
907                     
908                           .OpBSign_SI(div_op_a_signed),
909                           .OpCode_SI (operator_i[1:0]),
910                     
911                           .Res_DO(result_div),
912                     
913                           // Hand-Shake
914                           .InVld_SI (div_valid),
915                           .OutRdy_SI(ex_ready_i),
916                           .OutVld_SO(div_ready)
917                       );
918                     
919                       ////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
920                       //   ____                 _ _     __  __              //
921                       //  |  _ \ ___  ___ _   _| | |_  |  \/  |_   ___  __  //
922                       //  | |_) / _ \/ __| | | | | __| | |\/| | | | \ \/ /  //
923                       //  |  _ <  __/\__ \ |_| | | |_  | |  | | |_| |>  <   //
924                       //  |_| \_\___||___/\__,_|_|\__| |_|  |_|\__,_/_/\_\  //
925                       //                                                    //
926                       ////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
927                     
928                       always_comb begin
929        1/1              result_o = '0;
930                     
931        1/1              unique case (operator_i)
932                           // Standard Operations
933        1/1                ALU_AND: result_o = operand_a_i & operand_b_i;
934        1/1                ALU_OR:  result_o = operand_a_i | operand_b_i;
935        1/1                ALU_XOR: result_o = operand_a_i ^ operand_b_i;
936                     
937                           // Shift Operations
938                           ALU_ADD, ALU_ADDR, ALU_ADDU, ALU_ADDUR,
939                           ALU_SUB, ALU_SUBR, ALU_SUBU, ALU_SUBUR,
940                           ALU_SLL,
941                           ALU_SRL, ALU_SRA,
942                           ALU_ROR:
943        1/1                result_o = shift_result;
944                     
945                           // bit manipulation instructions
946        1/1                ALU_BINS, ALU_BEXT, ALU_BEXTU: result_o = bextins_result;
947                     
948        1/1                ALU_BCLR: result_o = bclr_result;
949        1/1                ALU_BSET: result_o = bset_result;
950                     
951                           // Bit reverse instruction
952        1/1                ALU_BREV: result_o = reverse_result;
953                     
954                           // pack and shuffle operations
955        0/1     ==>        ALU_SHUF, ALU_SHUF2, ALU_PCKLO, ALU_PCKHI, ALU_EXT, ALU_EXTS, ALU_INS: result_o = pack_result;
956                     
957                           // Min/Max/Ins
958        0/1     ==>        ALU_MIN, ALU_MINU, ALU_MAX, ALU_MAXU: result_o = result_minmax;
959                     
960                           //Abs/Cplxconj , ABS is used to do 0 - A for Cplxconj
961        0/1     ==>        ALU_ABS: result_o = is_clpx_i ? {adder_result[31:16], operand_a_i[15:0]} : result_minmax;
962                     
963        0/1     ==>        ALU_CLIP, ALU_CLIPU: result_o = clip_result;
964                     
965                           // Comparison Operations
966                           ALU_EQ, ALU_NE, ALU_GTU, ALU_GEU, ALU_LTU, ALU_LEU, ALU_GTS, ALU_GES, ALU_LTS, ALU_LES: begin
967        0/1     ==>          result_o[31:24] = {8{cmp_result[3]}};
968        0/1     ==>          result_o[23:16] = {8{cmp_result[2]}};
969        0/1     ==>          result_o[15:8]  = {8{cmp_result[1]}};
970        0/1     ==>          result_o[7:0]   = {8{cmp_result[0]}};
971                           end
972                           // Non-vector comparisons
973        0/1     ==>        ALU_SLTS, ALU_SLTU, ALU_SLETS, ALU_SLETU: result_o = {31'b0, comparison_result_o};
974                     
975        0/1     ==>        ALU_FF1, ALU_FL1, ALU_CLB, ALU_CNT: result_o = {26'h0, bitop_result[5:0]};
976                     
977                           // Division Unit Commands
978        1/1                ALU_DIV, ALU_DIVU, ALU_REM, ALU_REMU: result_o = result_div;
979                     
980        1/1                default: ;  // default case to suppress unique warning
